NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

1723. Thiru Kuppuraju, P., (Hindu), son of Thiru
Paramasivam, born on 2nd April 1985 (native district: Salem),
residing at No. 3-9/10, Sangari Main Road, Tharamangalam,
Omalur Taluk, Salem District, has converted to Christianity
with the name of JOSHUAH on 26th December 2008.
KUPPURAJU, P.
Tharamangalam, 17th April 2015.
1724. Thiru Mani (Hindu), son of Thiru Vetha Muthu,
born on 10th November 1979 (native district: The Nilgiris),
residing at No. 206, Summer House Road, Udhagamandalam,
The Nilgiris-643 001, has converted to Christianity with the
name of DAVID MANI on 25th July 1998.
MANI.
Udhagamandalam, 17th April 2015.
